# SDD Work Index

> Generated by `scripts/regen_sdd_work_index.py`. Do not hand-edit.

This index is a coordination board for coding agents. SDD artifacts are execution records; canonical project truth remains in code, root governance docs, domain architecture maps, tests, and generated contracts.

## Summary

| State | Features | Artifacts |
|-------|----------|-----------|
| `active` | 3 | 12 |
| `completed` | 3 | 12 |

## Lifecycle Flags

| Flag | Count | Meaning |
|------|-------|---------|
| `review-lifecycle` | 0 | Artifact status is not valid for its lane. |
| `artifact-status-mismatch` | 0 | Feature artifacts disagree on one lifecycle status. |
| `missing-status` | 0 | Artifact is missing a status line in its first 40 lines. |
| `missing-artifact` | 0 | Feature directory does not contain the full SDD artifact set. |
| `unexpected-artifact` | 0 | Feature directory contains files outside the four canonical artifacts. |
| `feature-slug-invalid` | 0 | Feature directory slug or artifact Date metadata is not machine-valid. |
| `spec-background-uncited` | 0 | Spec Background contains claims without repo path:line citations or https sources. |
| `worktree-metadata-invalid` | 0 | Worktree and Branch metadata are malformed or inconsistent. |
| `plan-preflight-metadata-mismatch` | 0 | Checked plan pre-flight Worktree/Branch claims disagree with metadata. |
| `plan-analyze-gate-invalid` | 0 | Plan Analyze Gate result cells use invalid status tokens. |
| `artifact-owning-link-mismatch` | 0 | Artifact owning links do not point at the same feature's canonical files. |
| `missing-gate-section` | 0 | Artifact is missing required clarify, checklist, analyze, task, or verification sections. |
| `duplicate-gate-section` | 0 | Artifact repeats required clarify, checklist, analyze, task, or verification sections. |
| `gate-evidence-missing` | 0 | Required SDD gate sections lack non-placeholder structured evidence rows. |
| `metadata-date-invalid` | 0 | Artifact Date or Approved at metadata is not a canonical YYYY-MM-DD real date. |
| `acceptance-numbering-invalid` | 0 | Spec or plan acceptance criteria are not unique contiguous AC numbers. |
| `acceptance-criterion-format-invalid` | 0 | Spec acceptance criteria are not in executable WHEN/THEN/SHALL form. |
| `acceptance-command-invalid` | 0 | Plan acceptance entries are not command-shaped executable commands. |
| `acceptance-command-mismatch` | 0 | Plan acceptance commands do not exactly cover spec acceptance criteria. |
| `missing-approval-metadata` | 0 | Artifact lacks machine-readable approval or execution metadata. |
| `task-missing-coordination-fields` | 0 | Task records lack owner, touch set, conflict set, verification, review, or status fields. |
| `task-invalid-coordination-fields` | 0 | Task records contain non-path touch/file fields, non-command verification, invalid status, or malformed conflict rules. |
| `task-invalid-numbering` | 0 | Task headings are missing unique contiguous Task numbers. |
| `task-invalid-dependencies` | 0 | Task dependencies reference missing task numbers, unsupported syntax, or incomplete prerequisites. |
| `task-missing-agent-loop-fields` | 0 | Task records lack factory lane, deterministic constraints, on-demand context, kill criteria, or eval signal. |
| `task-invalid-agent-loop-fields` | 0 | Task agent-loop fields use invalid lane tokens or semantics. |
| `task-missing-review-fields` | 0 | Task records lack subagent report or parent review result evidence. |
| `task-invalid-review-fields` | 0 | Task report/review evidence is inconsistent with delegation, scope, or status. |
| `task-complete-missing-review-evidence` | 0 | Completed task lacks explicit parent-reviewed or accepted review evidence. |
| `task-missing-subagent-handoff-artifact` | 0 | Delegated task references a subagent handoff artifact that is missing. |
| `task-invalid-subagent-handoff-artifact` | 0 | Delegated task references a subagent handoff artifact that is not bound to the task. |
| `task-missing-subagent-report-artifact` | 0 | Delegated task references a subagent report artifact that is missing. |
| `task-invalid-subagent-report-artifact` | 0 | Delegated task report artifact fails the task-bound report validator. |
| `task-complete-missing-failing-test-evidence` | 0 | Completed task lacks successful verification evidence covering its failing-test-first references. |
| `task-complete-missing-verification-evidence` | 0 | Completed task lacks matching verification command evidence with exit code 0. |
| `task-incomplete-in-verified-feature` | 0 | Verified feature contains incomplete task status. |
| `tasks-final-verification-duplicated` | 0 | tasks.md keeps a duplicate Final verification checklist instead of delegating final evidence to verification.md. |
| `verification-status-token-invalid` | 0 | Verification tables use non-machine-readable status tokens. |
| `verified-missing-check-all` | 0 | Verified record lacks successful make check-all evidence. |
| `verified-extra-verification-command` | 0 | Verified record includes commands other than make check-all in final Verification commands evidence. |
| `verified-extra-verification-output` | 0 | Verified record includes extra fenced transcript output in final Verification commands evidence. |
| `verified-missing-spec-compliance-evidence` | 0 | Verified spec compliance rows reference commands without matching exit code 0 evidence. |
| `verified-incomplete-spec-compliance` | 0 | Verified record lacks complete Spec compliance rows for every acceptance criterion. |
| `verified-coverage-incomplete` | 0 | Verified record lacks complete concrete coverage evidence. |
| `verified-e2e-incomplete` | 0 | Verified record lacks every required checked E2E golden-path signal. |
| `verified-contradicts-evidence` | 0 | Verified record contains text that contradicts final evidence. |
| `verified-unexplained-skips` | 0 | Verified record contains skipped tests or lacks numeric zero-skip evidence. |
| `superseded-missing-successor` | 0 | Superseded record lacks a machine-readable existing successor path. |
| `superseded-successor-mismatch` | 0 | Superseded artifacts in one feature disagree on the successor. |
| `active-touch-conflict` | 0 | Active features share touch paths without an explicit coordination rule. |
| `active-feature-too-large` | 0 | Active feature has too many task records for a bounded agent loop. |
| `active-sdd-lifecycle-check-flag-invalid` | 0 | Active records advertise obsolete SDD lifecycle --check flags. |
| `active-placeholder-final-evidence` | 0 | Active records contain placeholder final verification transcripts. |
| `active-skipped-count-without-final-evidence` | 0 | Active records claim numeric skipped-test counts without final make check-all evidence. |
